VALUES (@p0, @p1, @p2, @p3, @p4, @p5, @p6, @p7, @p8, @p9, @p10, @p11, @p12, @p13, @p14, @p15, @p16, @p17, @p18, @p19, @p20, @p21, 0)) AS i ([C_Org_Id], [CreatedUser], [Golf_Address], [Golf_CardNo], [Golf_CardStatus], [Golf_CardType], [Golf_DOB], [Golf_Effective_Date], [Golf_Email], [Golf_Expire_Date], [Golf_FullName], [Golf_IDNo], [Golf_IsActive], [Golf_IsLock], [Golf_MemberCardId], [Golf_Mobilephone], [IsActive], [IsDelete], [MB_CustomerGroup_Id], [MB_Customer_Id], [UpdatedDate], [UpdatedUser], _Position) ON 1=0
WHEN NOT MATCHED THEN
INSERT ([C_Org_Id], [CreatedUser], [Golf_Address], [Golf_CardNo], [Golf_CardStatus], [Golf_CardType], [Golf_DOB], [Golf_Effective_Date], [Golf_Email], [Golf_Expire_Date], [Golf_FullName], [Golf_IDNo], [Golf_IsActive], [Golf_IsLock], [Golf_MemberCardId], [Golf_Mobilephone], [IsActive], [IsDelete], [MB_CustomerGroup_Id], [MB_Customer_Id], [UpdatedDate], [UpdatedUser])
VALUES (i.[C_Org_Id], i.[CreatedUser], i.[Golf_Address], i.[Golf_CardNo], i.[Golf_CardStatus], i.[Golf_CardType], i.[Golf_DOB], i.[Golf_Effective_Date], i.[Golf_Email], i.[Golf_Expire_Date], i.[Golf_FullName], i.[Golf_IDNo], i.[Golf_IsActive], i.[Golf_IsLock], i.[Golf_MemberCardId], i.[Golf_Mobilephone], i.[IsActive], i.[IsDelete], i.[MB_CustomerGroup_Id], i.[MB_Customer_Id], i.[UpdatedDate], i.[UpdatedUser])
OUTPUT INSERTED.[Id], i._Position
INTO @inserted0;

SELECT [t].[Id], [t].[CreatedDate] FROM [MB_MemberCard] t
INNER JOIN @inserted0 i ON ([t].[Id] = [i].[Id])
ORDER BY [i].[_Position];"
